I've uploaded a code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
re-add --re-encrypt: secret scanner warns on files that are already encrypted in source
## Summary

When running `chezmoi re-add --re-encrypt`, the secret scanner (`add.secrets: warning`) emits warnings for files that already have the `encrypted_` prefix in the source state. Since these files are stored as age-encrypted blobs in git, the secrets are not actually exposed.

## Steps to reproduce

1. Add a file containing an API key with encryption:
   ```
   chezmoi add --encrypt ~/.config/some-tool/config.toml
   ```
2. Modify the target file
3. Re-add with re-encryption:
   ```
   chezmoi re-add --re-encrypt
   ```

## Expected behavior

No warning for files that already have the `encrypted_` attribute in source state, since the plaintext never reaches git.

## Actual behavior

```
chezmoi: /home/user/.config/some-tool/config.toml:97: Detected a Generic API Key, potentially exposing access to various services and sensitive operations.
```

The operation succeeds (with `warning` mode), but the warning is misleading — it suggests the key is being exposed when it's actually about to be encrypted.

With `add.secrets: error`, this blocks `re-add --re-encrypt` entirely (exit code 1), making `error` mode unusable for repos with encrypted secrets.

## Question

Is this by design? Should the scanner skip files that already have the `encrypted_` source state attribute, or is there a recommended workflow I'm missing?

## Environment

- chezmoi v2.70.0
- encryption: age
- `add.secrets` at default (`warning`)

</pr_description>

    84	func (c *Config) defaultOnIgnoreFunc(targetRelPath chezmoi.RelPath) {
    85	        if !c.Add.quiet {
    86	                c.errorf("warning: ignoring %s\n", targetRelPath)
    87	        }
    88	}
    89	
    90	func (c *Config) defaultPreAddFunc(targetRelPath chezmoi.RelPath, fileInfo fs.FileInfo) error {
    91	        // Scan unencrypted files for secrets, if configured.
    92	        if c.Add.Secrets.String() != severityIgnore && fileInfo.Mode().Type() == 0 && !c.Add.Encrypt {
    93	                absPath := c.DestDirAbsPath.Join(targetRelPath)
    94	                content, err := c.destSystem.ReadFile(absPath)
    95	                if err != nil {
    96	                        return err
    97	                }
    98	                gitleaksDetector, err := c.getGitleaksDetector()
    99	                if err != nil {
   100	                        return err
   101	                }
   102	                findings := gitleaksDetector.DetectBytes(content)
   103	                for _, finding := range findings {
   104	                        c.errorf("%s:%d: %s\n", absPath, finding.StartLine+1, finding.Description)
   105	                }
   106	                if !c.force && c.Add.Secrets.String() == severityError && len(findings) > 0 {
   107	                        return chezmoi.ExitCodeError(1)
   108	                }
   109	        }
   110	
   111	        if !c.Add.prompt {
   112	                return nil
   113	        }
   114	
   115	        prompt := fmt.Sprintf("add %s", c.SourceDirAbsPath.Join(targetRelPath))
   116	        for {
   117	                switch choice, err := c.promptChoice(prompt, choicesYesNoAllQuit); {
   118	                case err != nil:
   119	                        return err
   120	                case choice == "all":
   121	                        c.Add.prompt = false
   122	                        return nil
   123	                case choice == "no":
   124	                        return fs.SkipDir
   125	                case choice == "quit":
   126	                        return chezmoi.ExitCodeError(0)
   127	                case choice == "yes":
   128	                        return nil
   129	                default:
   130	                        panic(choice + ": unexpected choice")
   131	                }
   132	        }
   133	}
   134	
   135	// defaultReplaceFunc prompts the user for confirmation if the adding the entry
   136	// would remove any of the encrypted, private, or template attributes.
   137	func (c *Config) defaultReplaceFunc(
   138	        targetRelPath chezmoi.RelPath,
   139	        newSourceStateEntry, oldSourceStateEntry chezmoi.SourceStateEntry,
   140	) error {
   141	        if c.force {
   142	                return nil
   143	        }
   144	
   145	        newFile, newIsFile := newSourceStateEntry.(*chezmoi.SourceStateFile)
   146	        oldFile, oldIsFile := oldSourceStateEntry.(*chezmoi.SourceStateFile)
   147	        if !newIsFile || !oldIsFile {
   148	                return nil
   149	        }
   150	
   151	        var removedAttributes []string
   152	        if !newFile.Attr().Encrypted && oldFile.Attr().Encrypted {
   153	                removedAttributes = append(removedAttributes, "encrypted")
   154	        }
   155	        if !newFile.Attr().Private && oldFile.Attr().Private {
   156	                removedAttributes = append(removedAttributes, "private")
   157	        }
   158	        if !newFile.Attr().Template && oldFile.Attr().Template {
   159	                removedAttributes = append(removedAttributes, "template")
   160	        }
   161	        if len(removedAttributes) == 0 {
   162	                return nil
   163	        }
   164	        removedAttributesStr := englishListWithNoun(removedAttributes, "attribute", "")
   165	        prompt := fmt.Sprintf("adding %s would remove %s, continue", targetRelPath, removedAttributesStr)
   166	
   167	        for {
   168	                switch choice, err := c.promptChoice(prompt, choicesYesNoAllQuit); {
   169	                case err != nil:
   170	                        return err
   171	                case choice == "all":
   172	                        c.force = true
   173	                        return nil
   174	                case choice == "no":
   175	                        return fs.SkipDir
   176	                case choice == "quit":
   177	                        return chezmoi.ExitCodeError(0)
   178	                case choice == "yes":
   179	                        return nil
   180	                default:

    66	func (c *Config) runReAddCmd(cmd *cobra.Command, args []string, sourceState *chezmoi.SourceState) error {
    67	        var targetRelPaths []chezmoi.RelPath
    68	        sourceStateEntries := make(map[chezmoi.RelPath]chezmoi.SourceStateEntry)
    69	        if len(args) == 0 {
    70	                _ = sourceState.ForEach(
    71	                        func(targetRelPath chezmoi.RelPath, sourceStateEntry chezmoi.SourceStateEntry) error {
    72	                                targetRelPaths = append(targetRelPaths, targetRelPath)
    73	                                sourceStateEntries[targetRelPath] = sourceStateEntry
    74	                                return nil
    75	                        },
    76	                )
    77	        } else {
    78	                var err error
    79	                targetRelPaths, err = c.targetRelPaths(sourceState, args, targetRelPathsOptions{
    80	                        recursive: c.reAdd.recursive,
    81	                })
    82	                if err != nil {
    83	                        return err
    84	                }
    85	                for _, targetRelPath := range targetRelPaths {
    86	                        sourceStateEntries[targetRelPath] = sourceState.Get(targetRelPath)
    87	                }
    88	        }
    89	        slices.SortFunc(targetRelPaths, chezmoi.CompareRelPaths)
    90	
    91	        // Track which files were already processed to avoid double-processing with exact directories
    92	        processedFiles := make(map[chezmoi.RelPath]bool)
    93	
    94	TARGET_REL_PATH:
    95	        for _, targetRelPath := range targetRelPaths {
    96	                sourceStateFile, ok := sourceStateEntries[targetRelPath].(*chezmoi.SourceStateFile)
    97	                if !ok {
    98	                        continue
    99	                }
   100	                if sourceStateFile.Attr().Template {
   101	                        continue
   102	                }
   103	                if sourceStateFile.Attr().Type != chezmoi.SourceFileTypeFile {
   104	                        continue
   105	                }
   106	
   107	                destAbsPath := c.DestDirAbsPath.Join(targetRelPath)
   108	                destAbsPathInfo, err := c.destSystem.Stat(destAbsPath)
   109	                actualState, err := chezmoi.NewActualStateEntry(c.destSystem, destAbsPath, destAbsPathInfo, err)
   110	                if err != nil {
   111	                        return err
   112	                }
   113	                actualStateFile, ok := actualState.(*chezmoi.ActualStateFile)
   114	                if !ok {
   115	                        continue
   116	                }
   117	
   118	                targetState, err := sourceStateFile.TargetStateEntry(c.destSystem, c.DestDirAbsPath)
   119	                if err != nil {
   120	                        return err
   121	                }
   122	                targetStateFile, ok := targetState.(*chezmoi.TargetStateFile)
   123	                if !ok {
   124	                        continue
   125	                }
   126	
   127	                actualContents, err := actualStateFile.Contents()
   128	                if err != nil {
   129	                        return err
   130	                }
   131	                targetContents, err := targetStateFile.Contents()
   132	                if err != nil {
   133	                        return err
   134	                }
   135	
   136	                bytesEqual := bytes.Equal(actualContents, targetContents)
   137	                // On Windows, ignore permission changes as they are not preserved
   138	                // by the filesystem. On other systems, if there are no permission
   139	                // changes, continue.
   140	                //
   141	                // See https://github.com/twpayne/chezmoi/issues/3891.
   142	                permsEqual := runtime.GOOS == "windows" || actualStateFile.Perm() == targetStateFile.Perm(c.Umask)
   143	                reEncrypt := sourceStateFile.Attr().Encrypted && c.reAdd.reEncrypt
   144	                if bytesEqual && permsEqual && !reEncrypt {
   145	                        continue
   146	                }
   147	
   148	                if c.Interactive {
   149	                        prompt := fmt.Sprintf("Re-add %s", targetRelPath)
   150	                        var choices []string
   151	                        if actualContents != nil || targetContents != nil {
   152	                                choices = append(choices, "diff")
   153	                        }
   154	                        choices = append(choices, choicesYesNoAllQuit...)
   155	                FOR:
   156	                        for {
   157	                                switch choice, err := c.promptChoice(prompt, choices); {
   158	                                case err != nil:
   159	                                        return err
   160	                                case choice == "diff":
   161	                                        if err := c.diffFile(
   162	                                                targetRelPath,
   163	                                                c.SourceDirAbsPath.Join(sourceStateFile.SourceRelPath().RelPath()), targetContents, targetStateFile.Perm(c.Umask),
   164	                                                destAbsPath, actualContents, actualStateFile.Perm(),
   165	                                        ); err != nil {
   166	                                                return err
   167	                                        }
   168	                                case choice == "yes":
   169	                                        break FOR
   170	                                case choice == "no":
   171	                                        continue TARGET_REL_PATH
   172	                                case choice == "all":
   173	                                        c.Interactive = false
   174	                                        break FOR
   175	                                case choice == "quit":
   176	                                        return chezmoi.ExitCodeError(0)
   177	                                default:
   178	                                        panic(choice + ": unexpected choice")
   179	                                }
   180	                        }
   181	                }
   182	
   183	                // On Windows, as the file mode is not preserved by the filesystem, copy
   184	                // the existing mode from the target file. Hack this in by replacing the
   185	                // io/fs.FileInfo of the destination file with a new io/fs.FileInfo with
   186	                // the mode of the target file.
   187	                //
   188	                // See https://github.com/twpayne/chezmoi/issues/3891.
   189	                if runtime.GOOS == "windows" {
   190	                        destAbsPathInfo = &fileInfo{
   191	                                name:    destAbsPathInfo.Name(),
   192	                                size:    destAbsPathInfo.Size(),
   193	                                mode:    targetStateFile.Perm(0), // Use the mode from the target.
   194	                                modTime: destAbsPathInfo.ModTime(),
   195	                        }
   196	                }
   197	
   198	                destAbsPathInfos := map[chezmoi.AbsPath]fs.FileInfo{
   199	                        destAbsPath: destAbsPathInfo,
   200	                }
   201	                if err := sourceState.Add(c.sourceSystem, c.persistentState, c.destSystem, destAbsPathInfos, &chezmoi.AddOptions{
   202	                        Encrypt:         sourceStateFile.Attr().Encrypted,
   203	                        EncryptedSuffix: c.encryption.EncryptedSuffix(),
   204	                        Errorf:          c.errorf,
   205	                        Filter:          c.reAdd.filter,
   206	                        PreAddFunc:      c.defaultPreAddFunc,
   207	                }); err != nil {
   208	                        return err
   209	                }
   210	                // Mark this file as processed
   211	                processedFiles[targetRelPath] = true
   212	        }
   213	
   214	        // Process exact directories - add new files and remove deleted files
   215	        return c.processExactDirs(sourceState, sourceStateEntries, processedFiles)
   216	}
   217	
   218	// processExactDirs handles exact directory synchronization during re-add.
   219	// It adds new files found in exact target directories and removes files from
   220	// source that no longer exist in exact target directories.
   221	// processedFiles contains files that were already re-added in the file loop,
   222	// outside of the exact directory logic, to avoid double-processing them.
   223	func (c *Config) processExactDirs(
   224	        sourceState *chezmoi.SourceState,
   225	        sourceStateEntries map[chezmoi.RelPath]chezmoi.SourceStateEntry,
   226	        processedFiles map[chezmoi.RelPath]bool,
   227	) error {
   228	        // Collect all exact directories from source state that are in scope
   229	        // An exact directory is in scope if:
   230	        // 1. It's directly in sourceStateEntries (was explicitly or implicitly targeted)
   231	        // 2. Any of its children are in sourceStateEntries (parent dir needs sync)
   232	        exactDirs := make(map[chezmoi.RelPath]*chezmoi.SourceStateDir)
   233	
   234	        // First, collect exact directories that are directly in the entries
   235	        for targetRelPath, entry := range sourceStateEntries {
   236	                if sourceStateDir, ok := entry.(*chezmoi.SourceStateDir); ok && sourceStateDir.Attr().Exact {
   237	                        exactDirs[targetRelPath] = sourceStateDir
   238	                }
   239	        }
   240

   336	// A PreAddFunc is called before a new source state entry is added.
   337	type PreAddFunc func(targetRelPath RelPath, fileInfo fs.FileInfo) error
   338	
   339	// A ReplaceFunc is called before a source state entry is replaced.
   340	type ReplaceFunc func(targetRelPath RelPath, newSourceStateEntry, oldSourceStateEntry SourceStateEntry) error
   341	
   342	// AddOptions are options to SourceState.Add.
   343	type AddOptions struct {
   344	        AutoTemplate        bool                    // Automatically create templates, if possible.
   345	        Create              bool                    // Add create_ entries instead of normal entries.
   346	        Encrypt             bool                    // Encrypt files.
   347	        EncryptedSuffix     string                  // Suffix for encrypted files.
   348	        Errorf              func(string, ...any)    // Function to print errors.
   349	        Exact               bool                    // Add the exact_ attribute to added directories.
   350	        ExactTargetRelPaths chezmoiset.Set[RelPath] // Paths that should be marked exact (if nil and Exact is true, all dirs are exact).
   351	        Filter              *EntryTypeFilter        // Entry type filter.
   352	        OnIgnoreFunc        func(RelPath)           // Function to call when a target is ignored.
   353	        PreAddFunc          PreAddFunc              // Function to be called before a source entry is added.
   354	        ConfigFileAbsPath   AbsPath                 // Path to config file.
   355	        ProtectedAbsPaths   []AbsPath               // Paths that must not be added.
   356	        RemoveDir           RelPath                 // Directory to remove before adding.
   357	        ReplaceFunc         ReplaceFunc             // Function to be called before a source entry is replaced.
   358	        Template            bool                    // Add the .tmpl attribute to added files.
   359	        TemplateSymlinks    bool                    // Add symlinks with targets in the source or home directories as templates.
   360	}
   361	
   362	// shouldBeExact returns true if targetRelPath should have the exact attribute.
   363	// A path is exact if Exact is true AND either ExactTargetRelPaths is nil
   364	// (legacy behavior) or the path equals or is a descendant of an explicit
   365	// exact target.
   366	func (o *AddOptions) shouldBeExact(targetRelPath RelPath) bool {
   367	        if !o.Exact {
   368	                return false
   369	        }
   370	        // If ExactTargetRelPaths is nil, use legacy behavior (all dirs are exact)
   371	        if o.ExactTargetRelPaths == nil {
   372	                return true
   373	        }
   374	        // Check if targetRelPath equals or is a descendant of any exact target
   375	        for exactTarget := range o.ExactTargetRelPaths {
   376	                if targetRelPath == exactTarget || targetRelPath.HasDirPrefix(exactTarget) {
   377	                        return true
   378	                }
   379	        }
   380	        return false
   381	}
   382	
   383	// Add adds destAbsPathInfos to s.
   384	func (s *SourceState) Add(
   385	        sourceSystem System,
   386	        persistentState PersistentState,
   387	        destSystem System,
   388	        destAbsPathInfos map[AbsPath]fs.FileInfo,
   389	        options *AddOptions,
   390	) error {
   391	        // Filter out excluded and ignored paths.
   392	        destAbsPaths := slices.Sorted(maps.Keys(destAbsPathInfos))
   393	        n := 0
   394	        for _, destAbsPath := range destAbsPaths {
   395	                switch destAbsPathInfo := destAbsPathInfos[destAbsPath]; {
   396	                case destAbsPathInfo == nil:
   397	                        // If the destination does not exist then create a new, empty file,
   398	                        // unless files are excluded.
   399	                        if !options.Filter.IncludeEntryTypeBits(EntryTypeFiles) {
   400	                                continue
   401	                        }
   402	                case !options.Filter.IncludeFileInfo(destAbsPathInfo):
   403	                        continue
   404	                }
   405	
   406	                targetRelPath := destAbsPath.MustTrimDirPrefix(s.destDirAbsPath)
   407	                if s.Ignore(targetRelPath) {
   408	                        if options.OnIgnoreFunc != nil {
   409	                                options.OnIgnoreFunc(targetRelPath)
   410	                        }
   411	                        continue
   412	                }
   413	
   414	                destAbsPaths[n] = destAbsPath
   415	                n++
   416	        }
   417	        destAbsPaths = destAbsPaths[:n]
   418	
   419	        // Check for protected paths.
   420	        for _, destAbsPath := range destAbsPaths {
   421	                if destAbsPath == options.ConfigFileAbsPath {
   422	                        format := "%s: cannot add chezmoi's config file to chezmoi, use a config file template instead"
   423	                        return fmt.Errorf(format, destAbsPath)
   424	                }
   425	        }
   426	        for _, destAbsPath := range destAbsPaths {
   427	                for _, protectedAbsPath := range options.ProtectedAbsPaths {
   428	                        if protectedAbsPath.IsEmpty() {
   429	                                continue
   430	                        }
   431	                        if destAbsPath.HasDirPrefix(protectedAbsPath) {
   432	                                format := "%s: cannot add chezmoi file to chezmoi (%s is protected)"
   433	                                return fmt.Errorf(format, destAbsPath, protectedAbsPath)
   434	                        }
   435	                }
   436	        }
   437	
   438	        type sourceUpdate struct {
   439	                destAbsPath    AbsPath
   440	                entryState     *EntryState
   441	                sourceRelPaths []SourceRelPath
   442	        }
   443	
   444	        sourceUpdates := make([]sourceUpdate, 0, len(destAbsPaths))
   445	        newSourceStateEntries := make(map[SourceRelPath]SourceStateEntry)
   446	        newSourceStateEntriesByTargetRelPath := make(map[RelPath]SourceStateEntry)
   447	        nonEmptyDirs := chezmoiset.New[SourceRelPath]()
   448	        externalDirRelPaths := chezmoiset.New[RelPath]()
   449	        dirRenames := make(map[AbsPath]AbsPath)
   450	DEST_ABS_PATH:
   451	        for _, destAbsPath := range destAbsPaths {
   452	                targetRelPath := destAbsPath.MustTrimDirPrefix(s.destDirAbsPath)
   453	
   454	                // Skip any entries in known external dirs.
   455	                for externalDir := range externalDirRelPaths {
   456	                        if targetRelPath.HasDirPrefix(externalDir) {
   457	                                continue DEST_ABS_PATH
   458	                        }
   459	                }
   460	
   461	                // Find the target's parent directory in the source state.
   462	                var parentSourceRelPath SourceRelPath
   463	                if targetParentRelPath := targetRelPath.Dir(); targetParentRelPath == DotRelPath {
   464	                        parentSourceRelPath = SourceRelPath{}
   465	                } else if parentEntry, ok := newSourceStateEntriesByTargetRelPath[targetParentRelPath]; ok {
   466	                        parentSourceRelPath = parentEntry.SourceRelPath()
   467	                } else if nodes := s.root.GetNodes(targetParentRelPath); nodes != nil {
   468	                        for i, node := range nodes {
   469	                                if i == 0 {
   470	                                        // nodes[0].sourceStateEntry should always be nil because it
   471	                                        // refers to the destination directory, which is not managed.
   472	                                        // chezmoi manages the destination directory's contents, not
   473	                                        // the destination directory itself. For example, chezmoi
   474	                                        // does not set the name or permissions of the user's home
   475	                                        // directory.
   476	                                        if node.SourceStateEntry != nil {
   477	                                                panic(fmt.Errorf("nodes[0]: expected nil, got %+v", node.SourceStateEntry))
   478	                                        }
   479	                                        continue
   480	                                }
   481	                                switch sourceStateDir, ok := node.SourceStateEntry.(*SourceStateDir); {
   482	                                case i != len(nodes)-1 && !ok:
   483	                                        panic(fmt.Errorf("nodes[%d]: unexpected non-terminal source state entry, got %T", i, node.SourceStateEntry))
   484	                                case ok && sourceStateDir.attr.External:
   485	                                        targetRelPathComponents := targetRelPath.SplitAll()
   486	                                        externalDirRelPath := EmptyRelPath.Join(targetRelPathComponents[:i]...)
   487	                                        externalDirRelPaths.Add(externalDirRelPath)
   488	                                        if options.Errorf != nil {
   489	                                                options.Errorf("%s: skipping entries in external_ directory\n", externalDirRelPath)
   490	                                        }
   491	                                        continue DEST_ABS_PATH
   492	                                }
   493	                        }
   494	                        parentSourceRelPath = nodes[len(nodes)-1].SourceStateEntry.SourceRelPath()
   495	                } else {
   496	                        return fmt.Errorf("%s: parent directory not in source state", destAbsPath)
   497	                }
   498	                nonEmptyDirs.Add(parentSourceRelPath)
   499	
   500	                destAbsPathInfo := destAbsPathInfos[destAbsPath]
   501	                var actualStateEntry ActualStateEntry
   502	                var newSourceStateEntry SourceStateEntry
   503	                if destAbsPathInfo == nil {
   504	                        // If the destination does not exist then create a new, empty file.
   505	                        _, relPath := destAbsPath.Split()
   506	                        actualStateEntry = &ActualStateAbsent{
   507	                                absPath: destAbsPath,
   508	                        }
   509	                        fileAttr := FileAttr{
   510	                                TargetName: relPath.String(),
   511	                                Type:       SourceFileTypeFile,
   512	                                Encrypted:  options.Encrypt,
   513	                                Empty:      true,
   514	                                Template:   options.Template,
   515	                        }
   516	                        sourceRelPath := parentSourceRelPath.Join(NewSourceRelPath(fileAttr.SourceName(s.encryption.EncryptedSuffix())))
   517	                        newSourceStateEntry = &SourceStateFile{
   518	                                attr:          fileAttr,
   519	                                origin:        actualStateEntry,
   520	                                sourceRelPath: sourceRelPath,
   521	                                targetStateEntry: &TargetStateFile{
   522	                                        contentsFunc:       eagerZeroNoErr[[]byte](),
   523	                                        contentsSHA256Func: eagerNoErr(sha256.Sum256(nil)),
   524	                                        empty:              true,
   525	                                        perm:               0o666 &^ s.umask,
   526	                                },
   527	                        }
   528	                } else {
   529	                        var err error
   530	                        actualStateEntry, err = NewActualStateEntry(destSystem, destAbsPath, destAbsPathInfo, nil)
   531	                        if err != nil {
   532	                                return err
   533	                        }
   534	                        newSourceStateEntry, err = s.sourceStateEntry(actualStateEntry, destAbsPath, destAbsPathInfo, parentSourceRelPath, targetRelPath, options)
   535	                        if err != nil {
   536	                                return err
   537	                        }
   538	                        if newSourceStateEntry == nil {
   539	                                continue
   540	                        }
   541	                }
   542	
   543	                if options.PreAddFunc != nil && destAbsPathInfo != nil {
   544	                        switch err := options.PreAddFunc(targetRelPath, destAbsPathInfo); {
   545	                        case errors.Is(err, fs.SkipDir):
   546	                                continue DEST_ABS_PATH
   547	                        case err != nil:
   548	                                return err
   549	                        }
   550	                }
   551	
   552	                sourceEntryRelPath := newSourceStateEntry.SourceRelPath()
   553	
   554	                entryState, err := actualStateEntry.EntryState()
   555	                if err != nil {
   556	                        return err
   557	                }
   558	                update := sourceUpdate{
   559	                        destAbsPath:    destAbsPath,
   560	                        entryState:     entryState,
   561	                        sourceRelPaths: []SourceRelPath{sourceEntryRelPath},
   562	                }
   563	
   564	                if oldSourceStateEntry := s.root.Get(targetRelPath); oldSourceStateEntry != nil {
   565	                        oldSourceEntryRelPath := oldSourceStateEntry.SourceRelPath()
   566	                        if !oldSourceEntryRelPath.IsEmpty() && oldSourceEntryRelPath != sourceEntryRelPath {
   567	                                if options.ReplaceFunc != nil {
   568	                                        switch err := options.ReplaceFunc(targetRelPath, newSourceStateEntry, oldSourceStateEntry); {
   569	                                        case errors.Is(err, fs.SkipDir):
   570	                                                continue DEST_ABS_PATH

    34	// Decrypt implements Encryption.Decrypt.
    35	func (e *AgeEncryption) Decrypt(ciphertext []byte) ([]byte, error) {
    36	        if e.UseBuiltin {
    37	                return e.builtinDecrypt(ciphertext)
    38	        }
    39

    43	        return chezmoilog.LogCmdOutput(slog.Default(), cmd)

    96	// builtinDecrypt decrypts ciphertext using the builtin age.
    97	func (e *AgeEncryption) builtinDecrypt(ciphertext []byte) ([]byte, error) {
    98	        identities, err := e.builtinIdentities()
    99	        if err != nil {
   100	                return nil, err
   101	        }
   102	        var ciphertextReader io.Reader = bytes.NewReader(ciphertext)
   103	        if bytes.HasPrefix(ciphertext, []byte(armor.Header)) {
   104	                ciphertextReader = armor.NewReader(ciphertextReader)
   105	        }
   106	        plaintextReader, err := age.Decrypt(ciphertextReader, identities...)
   107	        if err != nil {
   108	                return nil, err
   109	        }
   110	        plaintextBuffer := &bytes.Buffer{}
   111	        if _, err := io.Copy(plaintextBuffer, plaintextReader); err != nil {
   112	                return nil, err
   113	        }
   114	        return plaintextBuffer.Bytes(), nil
   115	}
   116	
   117	// builtinEncrypt encrypts ciphertext using the builtin age.
   118	func (e *AgeEncryption) builtinEncrypt(plaintext []byte) ([]byte, error) {
   119	        recipients, err := e.builtinRecipients()
   120	        if err != nil {
   121	                return nil, err
   122	        }
   123	        ciphertextBuffer := &bytes.Buffer{}
   124	        armoredCiphertextWriter := armor.NewWriter(ciphertextBuffer)
   125	        ciphertextWriteCloser, err := age.Encrypt(armoredCiphertextWriter, recipients...)
   126	        if err != nil {
   127	                return nil, err
   128	        }
   129	        if _, err := io.Copy(ciphertextWriteCloser, bytes.NewReader(plaintext)); err != nil {
   130	                return nil, err
   131	        }
   132	        if err := ciphertextWriteCloser.Close(); err != nil {
   133	                return nil, err
   134	        }
   135	        if err := armoredCiphertextWriter.Close(); err != nil {
   136	                return nil, err
   137	        }
   138	        return ciphertextBuffer.Bytes(), nil
   139	}
   140	
   141	// builtinIdentities returns the identities for decryption using the builtin
   142	// age.
   143	func (e *AgeEncryption) builtinIdentities() ([]age.Identity, error) {
   144	        var identities []age.Identity
   145	        if !e.Identity.IsEmpty() {
   146	                parsedIdentities, err := parseIdentityFile(e.Identity)
   147	                if err != nil {
   148	                        return nil, err
   149	                }
   150	                identities = append(identities, parsedIdentities...)
   151	        }
   152	        for _, identityAbsPath := range e.Identities {
   153	                parsedIdentities, err := parseIdentityFile(identityAbsPath)
   154	                if err != nil {
   155	                        return nil, err
   156	                }
   157	                identities = append(identities, parsedIdentities...)
   158	        }
   159	        return identities, nil
   160	}

  3011	        if err != nil {
  3012	                return err
  3013	        }

  3028	// sourceStateEntry returns a new SourceStateEntry based on actualStateEntry.
  3029	func (s *SourceState) sourceStateEntry(
  3030	        actualStateEntry ActualStateEntry,
  3031	        destAbsPath AbsPath,
  3032	        fileInfo fs.FileInfo,
  3033	        parentSourceRelPath SourceRelPath,
  3034	        targetRelPath RelPath,
  3035	        options *AddOptions,
  3036	) (SourceStateEntry, error) {
  3037	        switch actualStateEntry := actualStateEntry.(type) {
  3038	        case *ActualStateAbsent:
  3039	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("%s: not found", destAbsPath)
  3040	        case *ActualStateDir:

  3047	                panic(fmt.Sprintf("%T: unsupported type", actualStateEntry))

   410	// cmdMkAgeConfig creates an age key and a chezmoi configuration file.
   411	func cmdMkAgeConfig(ts *testscript.TestScript, neg bool, args []string) {
   412	        if neg {
   413	                ts.Fatalf("unsupported: ! mkageconfig")
   414	        }
   415	        if len(args) > 1 || len(args) == 1 && args[0] != "-symmetric" {
   416	                ts.Fatalf("usage: mkageconfig [-symmetric]")
   417	        }
   418	        symmetric := len(args) == 1 && args[0] == "-symmetric"
   419	        homeDir := ts.Getenv("HOME")
   420	        ts.Check(os.MkdirAll(homeDir, fs.ModePerm))
   421	        identityFile := filepath.Join(homeDir, "key.txt")
   422	        recipient, err := chezmoitest.AgeGenerateKey("age", ts.MkAbs(identityFile))
   423	        ts.Check(err)
   424	        configFile := filepath.Join(homeDir, ".config", "chezmoi", "chezmoi.toml")
   425	        ts.Check(os.MkdirAll(filepath.Dir(configFile), fs.ModePerm))
   426	        lines := []string{
   427	                `encryption = "age"`,
   428	                `[age]`,
   429	                `    identity = ` + strconv.Quote(identityFile),
   430	        }
   431	        if symmetric {
   432	                lines = append(lines, `    symmetric = true`)
   433	        } else {
   434	                lines = append(lines, `    recipient = `+strconv.Quote(recipient.String()))
   435	        }
   436	        ts.Check(writeNewFile(configFile, []byte(chezmoitest.JoinLines(lines...)), 0o666))
   437	}

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -eu
repo=/testbed
tmp=$(mktemp -d)
export HOME="$tmp/home"
export XDG_CONFIG_HOME="$HOME/.config"
mkdir -p "$HOME/.config/chezmoi"
keyfile="$HOME/key.txt"

recipient=$(sed -n 's/^# public key: //p' "$keyfile")

encryption = "age"
useBuiltinAge = true

    identity = "$keyfile"
    recipient = "$recipient"
[add]
    secrets = "error"
CONFIG

AWS_ACCESS_KEY_ID=AKIALALEMEL33243OLIA
SECRET
# Adding encrypted files should not be blocked by secret scanning.

AWS_ACCESS_KEY_ID=AKIALALEMEL33244OLIA
SECRET
# Re-adding an already-encrypted file with --re-encrypt should not scan plaintext.
go run "$repo" re-add --re-encrypt --force
EOF

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -eu
tmp=$(mktemp -d)
export HOME="$tmp/home"
export XDG_CONFIG_HOME="$HOME/.config"
mkdir -p "$HOME/.config/chezmoi"
keyfile="$HOME/key.txt"
/tmp/chezmoi-repro age-keygen >"$keyfile"

encryption = "age"
useBuiltinAge = true
[age]
    identity = "$keyfile"
    recipient = "$recipient"
[add]
    secrets = "error"
CONFIG
cat >"$HOME/.secret" <<'SECRET'
AWS_ACCESS_KEY_ID=AKIALALEMEL33243OLIA
SECRET
/tmp/chezmoi-repro add --encrypt "$HOME/.secret"
cat >"$HOME/.secret" <<'SECRET'
AWS_ACCESS_KEY_ID=AKIALALEMEL33244OLIA
SECRET
/tmp/chezmoi-repro re-add --re-encrypt --force
EOF
